<time>1611899072722</time>< Review>
Last October my wife and I walked into the store on J st to sign up for a basic service plan with a promotional free phone. Duane, the store manager, was very friendly and professional as he assisted us, he listened to what we wanted and showed us the options of free phones with promotion. We thought this is simple and left feeling great. However, a series of problems followed us for months. Instead of the package we requested, he signed us up for a lease program.  It was a complete surprise to discover our two free phones were on monthly leases.  We didn't even know T-mobile had a lease program until we saw it on our second billing cycle.

Of course we reached out to Duane to correct the problem. Duane promised to follow up with the regional manager and get back to us. As you may expect, I did not received a call or email, nor did he return any of my calls or respond to my emails. This was two months of attempts to communicate with Duane, ZERO RESPONSE.  At the same time, I started working with the T-mobile support,  Duane ignored their multiple messagesas well.  Eventually, the problem was resolved through T-mobile customer service. Duane wasn't going to correct the problem, they decided to issue credit to cover the cost of lease of the phones.
Please proceed with caution. If you are signing up for a plan, I highly recommend  double checking your written contract prior to leaving the store. What I thought was a simple and straightforward purchase, instead resulted in months of phone calls with customers service.< /Review>

Wanted to try a different crepe in this area and choose this one for the cute presentation. Ordered a custom crepe:

Expresso ice cream with chocolate sauce, pudding, custard and whipped cream. Original crepe batter (optional green tea)

Every ingredient was delicious. It had a large amount of whipped cream but it helped balance out the sweetness of the ice cream. The chocolate sauce had small bits of chocolate which greatly helped the texture of the crepe since we ordered all soft ingredients.

There's only 3 tables in the storefront but there are plenty of seats throughout the mall.

Tip: You always need whipped cream. I thank the worker for asking us. CASH ONLY</Text>

<rate>4<//rate>< text>
Sooo cute. I think the crepes are good (not mind-blowing) but it's fun getting a crepe with a cute animal face on it. I got a strawberry cheesecake ice cream with whipped cream and a red bean add-on. The red bean was a bad idea and didn't meld.

The crepe itself is soft and chewy, which I really liked but I understand that others prefer a crispy crepe. It held up well, even after eating for a while - instead of getting my hands very sticky.

All in all, the face was adorable and made me smile but I kind of wish I had gotten the face-less banana and cream cheese crepe that they had on the menu. Next time!<//text>

<text>Come here if you want to instagram/snapchat/(add other social media) a picture of an adorable animal-shaped ice cream crepe. For a little over $5, you get a crepe with ice cream flavor + sauce of your choice adorned with other toppings to create an overly-cute animal face.

I got a green tea bear with marshmallow snout and fruit loop ears, and paired my ice cream with honey (one of my favorite combos is gt + honey). The crepe was warm, fresh and delicious, and all of the ingredients generally balanced well to make a not overly-sweet dessert. Other toppings such as fruit, having a green tea flavor batter, and sweets will run you a little extra, but they have tons of customization options. My simple crepe was still quite solid, and recommended as a photo-op and snack while taking a break from shopping in Japantown.<//text><GmapID>0x808580b8d7c745a3:0x8575070506231f69</GmapID>< Resp>

There's usually a long line everytime I come here but I had to take my sister and her boyfriend here. They loved the kawaii-ness of the crepe but was also surprised that the ice cream itself was good too. They almost did not want to eat it because it was too cute. They had the vanilla and green tea ice cream while I had the strawberry cheesecake one. They're all really creamy and good. The strawberry cheesecake actually had pieces of cheesecake in it. The line relatively goes by quickly and you get your stuff in good time as well. I think it was worth it if you're around Japantown.</Review>

Great experience with an excellent view and friendly staff. We tried multiple wine tastings in Napa and this was the best. We are not experts in wines and all we were looking for was a nice presentation, and a good history on what we were having. Chris was nice enough to cover all 5 wines (nothing orange, despite some other review I saw) and a brief history on the vineyards. As people who just wanted to have a good time with a nice view and outside seating (and not necessarily judging the quality of wine cuz I am by no means a wine enthusiast) we truly enjoyed the experience.<//review>

1618591752277</time>
<resp>None<//resp><Rate>5</Rate><username>akosioben</username>< Text>
What a solid gem in Napa. It is not on the main road, but it is very much worth the detour. We sat on their sun soaked patio looking over Napa and the serving staff was phenomenal. They sat down with us (masked and socially distanced) to explain the origins of the wines and why they were different. I am not the most knowledgeable regarding wine, but they were not at all condescending or pretentious when I asked questions unlike other wineries in Napa. What else was so different about RSV was that I loved ALL of the wines in the tastings. Usually I will like 2 maybe 3 of the 5 tastings but at RSV I could have bought a bottle of all 5. I even bought a bottle without trying it (their Rose) because I trusted their wines so much. I will definitely be returning and am seriously considering becoming a member.< /Text>

< Review>
RSV is a very nice boutique winery on the Silverado Trail. This is a smaller but very interesting Organic winery known for its reds. The founder (Robert Sinskey) is a famous ophthalmologist from Santa Monica, CA

After 20 years, Robert Sinskey‚Äôs philosophy is that ‚ÄúWine is not an athletic event‚Äù holds true to this day. His goal has always been to make ‚Äúpure wines of character that pair well with cuisine‚Äù.

Was pleasantly surprised at how warm and inviting this place was. It was easy to find, easy to make a reservation at, and the staff was friendly and warm.< /Review>

< text>
i have visited and left a glowing review on Yelp last year. But since my last visit, they changed the tasting fee which is now outrageous $45 per person. Yes, it includes a tiny delicious snack plate, but there is no reason to charge that much, even in Napa. I LOVE Sinskey wine, and the bottles are reasonably priced (for Napa). But the tasting fee is not cool. I expressed my sentiment to the nice people pouring wine and they both agreed that the new price is not something they personally agree with as well. So I actually left without tasting or buying. I hope the owners will rethink their approach. $20 fee with an optional $10 for snack would be the average Napa tasting fee structure.< /text>

< text>
At&t is able to engage in implicit theft via their associated business, directvnow:

If I could give 0 stars, I would. I opened a phone service with at&t back in March 2018, and I unknowingly got some kind of "free trial" with directvnow with it. I had no idea this was signed up under my name, that my bank information was given over to directvnow, and that I would be charged $35 - $40 every month after. I never used this service-- I never even knew how to while I had this account.

It was only after I closed my at&t account (for unrelated reasons) that I finally realized the directvnow charge was actually instigated by at&t. Somehow directvnow cannot locate any account with my information because is now closed-- and yet THEY STILL HAVE MY BANK INFORMATION and I'm STILL BEING CHARGED EVERY MONTH.

After changing my bank card three times-- STILL being charged from directvnow-- I actually have to close my bank account essentially because of unagreed terms and withheld explicit information on the part of at&t.

Essentially, at&t / directvnow stole from me, via bureaucratic technicalities. Seriously, how do you have my bank information for a monthly bill, and yet you cannot locate my account to cancel?

If you are with at&t or signing up, I strongly advise you look at their fine print agreements and your information they share with directvnow. Otherwise you may find yourself under theft every month, and having to close your bank account.<//text>
